Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 67, the Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) Command Module (CM) software for Apollo 12.

They have been adapted from sources files for Comanche 55, and updated via disassembly of binary dumps of original core rope memory modules, part numbers 2003972-1081, 2003972-1091, 2003972-1111, 2003972-1121, 2003972-1131, and 2003972-1141.

Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Comanche 67 are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

012627,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
012628,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
012629,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Comanche revision 067.
012630,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the flight
012631,000006:                                                                                                  ##              software for the Command Module's (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer
012632,000007:                                                                                                  ##              (AGC) for Apollo 12. No original listings of this program are
012633,000008:                                                                                                  ##              available; instead, this file was created via dissassembly of
012634,000009:                                                                                                  ##              dumps of Comanche 067 core rope modules and comparison with
012635,000010:                                                                                                  ##              other AGC programs.
012636,000011:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
012637,000012:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
012638,000013:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
012639,000014:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2023-08-16 MAS  Created from Comanche 055.
012640,000015:                                                                                                  ##              2024-05-13 MAS  Updated for Comanche 067.
012641,000016: 
012642,000017:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
012643,000018:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
012644,000019:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
012645,000020:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
012646,000021: 
012647,000022:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
012648,000023: 
012649,000024:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
012650,000025:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
012651,000026:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
012652,000027:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
012653,000028: 
012654,000029:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
012655,000030:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
012656,000031:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
012657,000032:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
012658,000033:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
012659,000034: 
012660,000035:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
012661,000036:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
012662,000037:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
012663,000038:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
012664,000039: 
012665,000040:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
012666,000041:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
012667,000042: 
012668,000043:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
012669,000044: 
012670,000045:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
012671,000046:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
012672,000047:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
012673,000048:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
012674,000049:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
012675,000050:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012676,000051: 
012677,000052:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
012678,000053:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
012679,000054:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
012680,000055:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012681,000056: 
012682,000057:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
012683,000058:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
012684,000059:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
012685,000060:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
012686,000061:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012687,000062: 
012688,000063:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
012689,000064: 
012690,000065:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
012691,000066:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
012692,000067:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
012693,000068:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
012694,000069:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
012695,000070:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
012696,000071:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
012697,000072:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
012698,000073:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
012699,000074:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
012700,000075:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
012701,000076:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
012702,000077:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
012703,000078: 
012704,000079:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
012705,000080:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
012706,000081:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012707,000082: 
012708,000083:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
012709,000084: 
012710,000085:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
012711,000086:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
012712,000087:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
012713,000088: 
012714,000089:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
012715,000090:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
012716,000091:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
012717,000092:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
012718,000093:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
012719,000094:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
012720,000095:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
012721,000096: 
012722,000097:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
012723,000098:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
012724,000099: 
012725,000100:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
012726,000101: 
012727,000102:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
012728,000103:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
012729,000104:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
012730,000105:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
012731,000106: 
012732,000107:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
012733,000108: 
012734,000109:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
012735,000110:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
012736,000111:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
012737,000112:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
012738,000113: 
012739,000114:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
012740,000115:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
012741,000116: 
012742,000117:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
012743,000118: 
012744,000119:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
012745,000120:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
012746,000121: 
012747,000122:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
012748,000123:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
012749,000124:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
012750,000125:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
012751,000126: 
012752,000127:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
012753,000128:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
012754,000129: 
012755,000130:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
012756,000131:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
012757,000132:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
012758,000133:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
012759,000134: 
012760,000135:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
012761,000136:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
012762,000137: 
012763,000138:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
012764,000139:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
012765,000140: 
012766,000141:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
012767,000142: 
012768,000143:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
012769,000144:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
012770,000145:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
012771,000146:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
012772,000147: 
012773,000148:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
012774,000149:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
012775,000150: 
012776,000151:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
012777,000152:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
012778,000153: 
012779,000154:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
012780,000155:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
012781,000156:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
012782,000157: 
012783,000158:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
012784,000159: 
012785,000160:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
012786,000161:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
012787,000162:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
012788,000163:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
012789,000164: 
012790,000165:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
012791,000166: 
012792,000167:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012793,000168: 
012794,000169:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
012795,000170:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
012796,000171:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
012797,000172:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
012798,000173:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
012799,000174:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
012800,000175:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
012801,000176:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
012802,000177:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
012803,000178:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012804,000179:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
012805,000180:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
012806,000181:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012807,000182:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
012808,000183:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
012809,000184:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
012810,000185:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
012811,000186:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
012812,000187:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
012813,000188:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
012814,000189:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
012815,000190:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
012816,000191:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
012817,000192:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
012818,000193:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
012819,000194:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
012820,000195:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
012821,000196:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
012822,000197:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
012823,000198:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
012824,000199:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
012825,000200:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
012826,000201:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
012827,000202:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
012828,000203:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
012829,000204: 
012830,000205:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012831,000206: 
012832,000207:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012833,000208:                                                                                                  # DSEXIT         =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
012834,000209:                                                                                                  # EXITEM         =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
012835,000210:                                                                                                  # BLANKRET       =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
012836,000211:                                                                                                  # WRDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
012837,000212:                                                                                                  # WDRET          =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
012838,000213:                                                                                                  # DECRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
012839,000214:                                                                                                  # 21/22REG       =       INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
012840,000215:                                                                                                  # UPDATRET       =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
012841,000216:                                                                                                  # CHAR           =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
012842,000217:                                                                                                  # ERCNT          =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
012843,000218:                                                                                                  # DECOUNT        =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
012844,000219:                                                                                                  # SGNON          =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
012845,000220:                                                                                                  # NOUNTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
012846,000221:                                                                                                  # DISTEM         =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
012847,000222:                                                                                                  # DECTEM         =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
012848,000223:                                                                                                  # SGNOFF         =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR +,- ON
012849,000224:                                                                                                  # NVTEMP         =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR NVSUB
012850,000225:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP1        =       VBUF +1         STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
012851,000226:                                                                                                  # HITEMIN        =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012852,000227:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
012853,000228:                                                                                                  # CODE           =       VBUF +2         FOR DSPIN
012854,000229:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP2        =       VBUF +2         STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
012855,000230:                                                                                                  # LOTEMIN        =       VBUF +2         TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012856,000231:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMIN+1.
012857,000232:                                                                                                  # MIXTEMP        =       VBUF +3         FOR MIXNOUN DATA
012858,000233:                                                                                                  # SIGNRET        =       VBUF +3         RETURN FOR +,- ON
012859,000234:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
012860,000235:                                                                                                  # ENTRET         =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
012861,000236:                                                                                                  # WDCNT          =       DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
012862,000237:                                                                                                  # INREL          =       DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X,Y,Z, REG )
012863,000238:                                                                                                  # DSPMMTEM       =       MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
012864,000239:                                                                                                  # MIXBR          =       MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
012865,000240:                                                                                                  # TEM1           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012866,000241:                                                                                                  # DSREL          =       TEM1            REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
012867,000242:                                                                                                  # TEM2           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012868,000243:                                                                                                  # DSMAG          =       TEM2            MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
012869,000244:                                                                                                  # IDADDTEM       =       TEM2            MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE
012870,000245:                                                                                                  # TEM3           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012871,000246:                                                                                                  # COUNT          =       TEM3            FOR DSPIN
012872,000247:                                                                                                  # TEM4           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012873,000248:                                                                                                  # LSTPTR         =       TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
012874,000249:                                                                                                  # RELRET         =       TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
012875,000250:                                                                                                  # FREERET        =       TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
012876,000251:                                                                                                  # DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
012877,000252:                                                                                                  # SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
012878,000253:                                                                                                  # SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
012879,000254:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012880,000255:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
012881,000256:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
012882,000257:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
012883,000258:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
012884,000259:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
012885,000260:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
012886,000261:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
012887,000262:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
012888,000263:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
012889,000264:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
012890,000265: 
012891,000266:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012892,000267: 
012893,000268:                                                                                                  #  ADDITIONAL TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012894,000269: 
012895,000270:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
012896,000271:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
012897,000272:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
012898,000273:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
012899,000274:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
012900,000275: 
012901,000276:                                                                                                  #  END OF ADDITIONAL TEMPS FOR PINBALL EXEC ACTION
012902,000277: 
012903,000278:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
012904,000279: 
012905,000280:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
012906,000281:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
012907,000282:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
012908,000283: 
012909,000284:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
012910,000285: 
012911,000286:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
012912,000287: 
012913,000288:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
012914,000289:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
012915,000290:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
012916,000291: 
012917,000292:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
012918,000293: 
012919,000294:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
012920,000295:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
012921,000296:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
012922,000297:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
012923,000298:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
012924,000299:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
012925,000300:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
012926,000301:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
012927,000302:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
012928,000303:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
012929,000304:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
012930,000305:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
012931,000306: 
012932,000307:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
012933,000308:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
012934,000309:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
012935,000310:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
012936,000311:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
012937,000312:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
012938,000313: 
012939,000314:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
012940,000315:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
012941,000316:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
012942,000317:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
012943,000318:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
012944,000319:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
012945,000320: 
012946,000321:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
012947,000322: 
012948,000323:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
012949,000324:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
012950,000325:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
012951,000326:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
012952,000327:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
012953,000328:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
012954,000329:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
012955,000330:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
012956,000331:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
012957,000332:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
012958,000333:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
012959,000334: 
012960,000335:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
012961,000336: 
012962,000337:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
012963,000338:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
012964,000339:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2  (24)
012965,000340:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2  (22)
012966,000341:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2  (20)
012967,000342:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)
012968,000343:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
012969,000344:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
012970,000345:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
012971,000346:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
012972,000347:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
012973,000348:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
012974,000349:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
012975,000350:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
012976,000351: 
012977,000352:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
012978,000353: 
012979,000354:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
012980,000355:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
012981,000356:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
012982,000357:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
012983,000358:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
012984,000359:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
012985,000360:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
012986,000361:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
012987,000362:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
012988,000363:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
012989,000364:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
012990,000365: 
012991,000366:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
012992,000367: 
012993,000368:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
012994,000369:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
012995,000370:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
012996,000371: 
012997,000372:                                                                                                  #  START OF EXECUTIVE SECTION OF PINBALL
012998,000373: 
012999,000374: 40,2000                                           BANK     40                                    
013000,000375: 40,2000                                           SETLOC   PINBALL1                              
013001,000376: 40,2000                                           BANK                                           
013002,000377: 
013003,000378: 40,2000                                           COUNT    40/PIN                                
013004,000379: 
013005,000380: 40,2000           35033        CHARIN             CAF      ONE                                   #  BLOCK DISPLAY SYST
013006,000381: 40,2001           57012                           XCH      DSPLOCK                               #  MAKE DSP SYST BUSY, BUT SAVE OLD
013007,000382: 40,2002           54115                           TS       21/22REG                              #  C(DSPLOCK) FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET.
013008,000383: 40,2003           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ALL KEYS EXCEPT ER TURN ON KR LITE IF
013009,000384: 40,2004           02006                           TC       +2                                    #  CADRSTOR IS FULL.  THIS REMINDS OPERATOR
013010,000385: 40,2005           02013                           TC       CHARIN2                               #  TO RE-ESTABLISH A FLASHING DISPLAY
013011,000386: 40,2006           42057                           CS       ELRCODE1                              #  WHICH HE HAS OBSCURED WITH DISPLAYS OF
013012,000387: 40,2007           60154                           AD       MPAC                                  #  HIS OWN (SEE REMARKS PRECEDING ROUTINE
013013,000388: 40,2010           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  VBRELDSP).
013014,000389: 40,2011           12013                           BZF      CHARIN2                               
013015,000390: 40,2012           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
013016,000391: 40,2013           56154        CHARIN2            XCH      MPAC                                  
013017,000392: 40,2014           54117                           TS       CHAR                                  
013018,000393: 40,2015           50000                           INDEX    A                                     
013019,000394: 40,2016           02017                           TC       +1                                    #    INPUT CODE      FUNCTION
013020,000395: 40,2017           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        0
013021,000396: 40,2020           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        1
013022,000397: 40,2021           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        2
013023,000398: 40,2022           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        3
013024,000399: 40,2023           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        4

013029,000404: 40,2030           02062                           TC       89TEST                                #        11              9

013031,000406: 40,2032           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        13
013032,000407: 40,2033           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        14
013033,000408: 40,2034           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        15
013034,000409: 40,2035           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        16
013035,000410: 40,2036           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        17
013036,000411: 40,2037           02074                           TC       NUM        -2                         #        20              0

013042,000417: 40,2045           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        26
013043,000418: 40,2046           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        27
013044,000419: 40,2047           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        30

013052,000427: 
013053,000428: 40,2057           00022        ELRCODE1           OCT      22                                    
013054,000429: 40,2060           04715        ENTERJMP           TC       POSTJUMP

013056,000431: 
013057,000432: 40,2062           10777        89TEST             CCS      DSPCOUNT                              
013058,000433: 40,2063           02067                           TC       +4                                    #  +
013059,000434: 40,2064           02067                           TC       +3                                    #  +0
013060,000435: 40,2065           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #  - BLOCK DATA IN IF DSPCOUNT IS - OR -0
013061,000436: 40,2066           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #  -0
013062,000437: 40,2067           36214                           CAF      THREE                                 
013063,000438: 40,2070           71000                           MASK     DECBRNCH                              
013064,000439: 40,2071           10000                           CCS      A

013066,000441: 40,2073           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #  IF DECBRNCH IS +0, REJECT 8 OR 9
013067,000442: 
013068,000443:                                                                                                  #  NUM ASSEMBLES OCTAL 3 BITS AT A TIME.  FOR DECIMAL IT CONVERTS INCOMING
013069,000444:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS A FRACTION, KEEPING RESULTS TO DP.
013070,000445:                                                                                                  #  OCTAL RESULTS ARE LEFT IN XREG, YREG, OR ZREG.  HI PART OF DEC IN XREG,
013071,000446:                                                                                                  #  YREG, ZREG.  THE LOW PARTS IN XREGLP, YREGLP, OR ZREGLP)
013072,000447:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH IS LEFT AT +0 FOR OCT, +1 FOR + DEC, +2 FOR - DEC.
013073,000448:                                                                                                  #  IF DSPCOUNT WAS LEFT -, NO MORE DATA IS ACCEPTED.
013074,000449: 
013075,000450: 40,2074           35035                           CAF      ZERO

013081,000456: 40,2102           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #  -0
013082,000457: 40,2103           02225                           TC       GETINREL

013668,001043: 41,2351           04715        GODSPALM           TC       POSTJUMP                              
013669,001044: 41,2352           61325                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
013670,001045: 
013671,001046:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
013672,001047: 
013673,001048:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
013674,001049:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
013675,001050:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
013676,001051:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
013677,001052:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
013678,001053: 
013679,001054:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
013680,001055:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
013681,001056: 
013682,001057:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
013683,001058: 
013684,001059:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
013685,001060:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
013686,001061:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
013687,001062: 
013688,001063:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
013689,001064:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
013690,001065:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
013691,001066:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
013692,001067:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
013693,001068:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
013694,001069: 
013695,001070:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
013696,001071:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
013697,001072:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
013698,001073: 
013699,001074:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
013700,001075:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
013701,001076: 
013702,001077:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
013703,001078:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
013704,001079: 
013705,001080:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
013706,001081: 
013707,001082:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
013708,001083:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
013709,001084:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
013710,001085:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
013711,001086:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
013712,001087: 
013713,001088:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
013714,001089:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
013715,001090:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
013716,001091: 
013717,001092:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
013718,001093:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
013719,001094: 
013720,001095:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
013721,001096:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
013722,001097: 
013723,001098:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
013724,001099: 
013725,001100: 41,2353           45032        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
013726,001101: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
013727,001102: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD

013914,001289:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING IS ATYPICAL SF ROUTINE.  IT USES MPAC.  LEAVES RESU

014230,001605: 
014231,001606:                                                                                                  #  THIS IS A SPECIAL PURPOSE VERB FOR DISPLAYING A DOUBLE PRECISION AGC
014232,001607:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS 10 DECIMAL DIGITS ON THE AGC DISPLAY PANEL.  IT CAN BE USED WITH
014233,001608:                                                                                                  #  ANY NOUN, EXCEPT MIXED NOUNS.  IT DISPLAYS THE CONTENTS
014234,001609:                                                                                                  #  OF THE REGISTER NOUNADD IS POINTING TO.  IF USED WITH NOUNS WHICH ARE
014235,001610:                                                                                                  #  INHERENTLY NOT DP SUCH AS THE CDU COUNTERS THE DISPLAY WILL BE GARBAGE.
014236,001611:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY IS IN R1 AND R2 ONLY WITH THE SIGN IN R1.

014259,001634:                                                                                                  #  LOAD VERBS            IF ALARM CONDITION IS DETECTED DURING EXECUTE,
014260,001635:                                                                                                  #  CHECK FAIL LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND ENDOFJOB.  IF ALARM CONDITION IS
014261,001636:                                                                                                  #  DETECTED DURING ENTER OF DATA, CHECK FAIL IS TURNED ON AND IT RECYCLES
014262,001637:                                                                                                  #  TO EXECUTE OF ORIGINAL LOAD VERB.  RECYCLE CAUSED BY          1) DECIMAL MACHINE
014263,001638:                                                                                                  #  CADR          2) MIXTURE OF OCTAL/DECIMAL DATA        3) OCTAL DATA INTO DECIMAL
014264,001639:                                                                                                  #  ONLY NOUN     4) DEC DATA INTO OCT ONLY NOUN          5) DATA TOO LARGE FOR SCALE
014265,001640:                                                                                                  #  6) FEWER THAN 3 DATA WORDS LOADED FOR HRS, MIN, SEC NOUN.8  (2)-(6) ALARM
014266,001641:                                                                                                  #  AND RECYCLE OCCUR AT FINAL ENTER OF SET.      (1) ALARM AND RECYCLE OCCUR AT
014267,001642:                                                                                                  #  ENTER OF CADR.

014823,002198: 42,3517           55041                           TS       VERBSAVE                              #   IN CASE OPERATOR EXECUTED A LOWER LOAD
014824,002199: 42,3520           04161                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #   VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
014825,002200: 42,3521                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
014826,002201: 
014827,002202:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
014828,002203:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
014829,002204:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
014830,002205:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
014831,002206:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
014832,002207: 
014833,002208:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
014834,002209:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
014835,002210:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
014836,002211:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
014837,002212:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
014838,002213:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
014839,002214:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
014840,002215: 
014841,002216:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
014842,002217:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
014843,002218:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
014844,002219: 
014845,002220:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
014846,002221:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
014847,002222: 
014848,002223:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
014849,002224:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
014850,002225: 
014851,002226:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

014977,002352: 
014978,002353:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
014979,002354:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  THE FCADR OF THE 
014980,002355:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN.  IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
014981,002356:                                                                                                  #  
014982,002357:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
014983,002358: 
014984,002359:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
014985,002360:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
014986,002361:                                                                                                  #        V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
014987,002362: 
014988,002363:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
014989,002364:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                             V27N01E(FCADR)E
014990,002365:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,     V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E     V27N01E(FCADR)E
014991,002366: 
014992,002367: 41,3353           34333        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
014993,002368: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
014994,002369: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
014995,002370: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
014996,002371: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
014997,002372: 41,3360           04731                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
014998,002373: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
014999,002374: 41,3362           05233        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

015379,002754:                                                                                                  #  LEAVE IT IN A, INHINT AND TC MPAC.
