015410,002785: 
015411,002786:                                                                                                  #  VBRESEQ WAKES ENDIDLE AT SAME LINE AS FINAL ENTER OF LOAD (L+3).
015412,002787:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
015413,002788:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE.  SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS, PLEASE PERFORM,
015414,002789:                                                                                                  #  OR PLEASE MARK VERBS BECAUSE THEY ALREADY USE L+3 IN ANOTHER CONTEXT.)
015415,002790: 
015416,002791: 40,3373           45035        VBRESEQ            CS       ZERO                                  #  MAKE IT LOOK LIKE DATA IN.
015417,002792: 40,3374           03350                           TC       VBPROC     +1                         
015418,002793: 
015419,002794:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
015420,002795:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
015421,002796: 
015422,002797:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015423,002798: 
015424,002799:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015425,002800: 
015426,002801:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015427,002802:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015428,002803:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015429,002804:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015430,002805: 
015431,002806:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015432,002807:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015433,002808:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015434,002809: 
015435,002810:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015436,002811:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015437,002812:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015438,002813:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015439,002814:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015440,002815:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015441,002816:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
015442,002817:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
015443,002818:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015444,002819:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015445,002820:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015446,002821: 
015447,002822: 40,3375           45031        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015448,002823: 40,3376           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015449,002824: 40,3377           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
015450,002825: 40,3400           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015451,002826: 40,3401           35016                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015452,002827: 40,3402           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015453,002828: 40,3403           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015454,002829: 40,3404           03413                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
015455,002830: 40,3405           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015456,002831: 40,3406           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015457,002832: 40,3407           03411                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015458,002833: 40,3410           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015459,002834: 40,3411           04715                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015460,002835: 40,3412           21272                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015461,002836: 40,3413           35035        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015462,002837: 40,3414           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015463,002838: 40,3415           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015464,002839: 40,3416           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015465,002840: 40,3417           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015466,002841: 40,3420           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015467,002842: 
015468,002843: 40,3421                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015469,002844: 
015470,002845:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
015471,002846:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015472,002847:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015473,002848:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015474,002849:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015475,002850: 
015476,002851:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015477,002852:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015478,002853:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015479,002854: 
015480,002855:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015481,002856:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015482,002857: 
015483,002858:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015484,002859:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015485,002860:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015486,002861:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
015487,002862:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015488,002863: 
015489,002864:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015490,002865:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015491,002866:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015492,002867:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015493,002868: 
015494,002869:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015495,002870:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015496,002871:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015497,002872:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015498,002873:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015499,002874:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015500,002875:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015501,002876: 
015502,002877:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015503,002878:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015504,002879: 
015505,002880:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015506,002881:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015507,002882: 
015508,002883:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015509,002884:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015510,002885: 
015511,002886:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015512,002887:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015513,002888:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015514,002889:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015515,002890:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015516,002891:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015517,002892:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015518,002893: 
015519,002894:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL
015520,002895:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015521,002896:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
015522,002897:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015523,002898:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015524,002899:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
015525,002900:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015526,002901:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
015527,002902:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
015528,002903:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
015529,002904: 
015530,002905:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
015531,002906:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
015532,002907: 
015533,002908:    4170                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
015534,002909: 
015535,002910:    4170                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
015536,002911: 
015537,002912:    4170           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
015538,002913:    4171           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP                                
015539,002914:    4172           35016                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015540,002915:    4173           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
015541,002916:    4174           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
015542,002917:    4175           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015543,002918:    4176           00002                           TC       Q                                     #  DSP SYST BLOCKED.  RET TO 1+ CALLING LOC
015544,002919:    4177           35033                           CAF      ONE                                   #  DSP SYST AVAILABLE
015545,002920:    4200           60002        NVSBCOM            AD       Q                                     
015546,002921:    4201           55037                           TS       NVQTEM                                #  2+ CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM
015547,002922:    4202           23022                           LXCH     MONSAVE2                              #  STORE NVMONOPT OPTIONS
015548,002923:    4203           04220                           TC       KILMONON                              #  TURN ON KILL MONITOR BIT

015563,002938: 
015564,002939:    4216           53040        NVSUBEND           DXCH     NVQTEM                                #  NVBNKTEM MUST = NVQTEM+1
015565,002940:    4217           05243                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
015566,002941:

015571,002946:                                                                                                  #  BLANKDSP BLANKS DISPLAY ACCORDING TO OPTION NUMBER IN NVTEMP AS FOLLOWS
015572,002947:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015573,002948:

015596,002971:

015602,002977: 41,3551           03516                           TC       BLANKDSP                              #  BLANK DISPLAY AS SPECIFIED
015603,002978: 41,3552           02351                           TC       GODSPALM

015607,002982: 41,3556           30123                           CA       NVTEMP                                #                 USES MPAC, +1, +2
015608,002983: 41,3557           54023                           TS       EDOP                                  #  RIGHT 7
015609,002984: 41,3560           30023                           CA       EDOP                                  
015610,002985: 41,3561           54160                           TS       MPAC       +4                         #  TEMP FOR VERB (CANT USE MPAC+1.  DSPDECVN
015611,002986:                                                                                                  #                 USES MPAC, +1, +2).
015612,002987: 41,3562           10157                           CCS      MPAC       +3                         #  TEST NOUN
015613,002988: 41,3563           03571                           TC       NVSUB2                                #  IF NOUN NOT +0, GO ON

015616,002991: 41,3566           35035                           CAF      ZERO                                  #  ZERO REQRET SO THAT PASTED VERBS CAN
015617,002992: 41,3567           55013                           TS       REQRET                                #  BE EXECUTED BY OPERATOR.
015618,002993: 41,3570           04216        ENTSET             TC       NVSUBEND                              
015619,002994: 41,3571           10160        NVSUB2             CCS      MPAC       +4                         #  TEST VERB
015620,002995: 41,3572           03576                           TC       +4                                    #  IF VERB NOT +0, GO ON
015621,002996: 41,3573           30157                           CA       MPAC       +3                         
015622,002997: 41,3574           02317                           TC       UPDATNN    -1                         #  IF VERB = +0, DISPLAY NOUN.  THEN RETURN
015623,002998: 41,3575           04216                           TC       NVSUBEND                              
015624,002999: 41,3576           30156                           CA       MPAC       +2                         #  TEMP FOR MACH CADR TO BE SPEC.  (DSPDECVN
015625,003000: 41,3577           54161                           TS       MPAC       +5                         #        USES MPAC, +1, +2)
015626,003001: 41,3600           30160                           CA       MPAC       +4                         
015627,003002: 41,3601           02337                           TC       UPDATVB    -1                         #  IF BOTH NOUN AND VERB NOT +0, DISPLAY
015628,003003: 41,3602           30157                           CA       MPAC       +3                         #  BOTH AND GO TO ENTPAS0.
015629,003004: 41,3603           02317                           TC       UPDATNN    -1                         
015630,003005: 41,3604           35035                           CAF      ZERO                                  
015631,003006: 41,3605           55014                           TS       LOADSTAT                              #  SET FOR WAITING FOR DATA CONDITION
015632,003007: 41,3606           55015                           TS       CLPASS

015634,003009: 41,3610           30161                           CA       MPAC       +5                         #  RESTORES MACH CADR TO BE SPEC TO MPAC+2
015635,003010: 41,3611           54156                           TS       MPAC       +2                         #  FOR USE IN INTMCTBS (IN ENTPAS0).

015637,003012: 
015638,003013:                                                                                                  #  IF INTERNAL MACH CADR TO BE SPECIFIED, MPAC+2 WILL BE PLACED INTO
015639,003014:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
015640,003015: 
015641,003016:    4220                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
015642,003017:    4220                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
015643,003018:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
015644,003019:    4220           35015        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
015645,003020:    4221           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
015646,003021:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
015647,003022:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
015648,003023: 
015649,003024:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
015650,003025:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
015651,003026:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE       SET BY SPECIAL VERB
015652,003027:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
015653,003028:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
015654,003029: 
015655,003030:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
015656,003031:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
015657,003032:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
015658,003033:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
015659,003034:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
015660,003035:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
015661,003036:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
015662,003037:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
015663,003038:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
015664,003039:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
015665,003040: 
015666,003041:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
015667,003042:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
015668,003043:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
015669,003044:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
015670,003045:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
015671,003046:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
015672,003047: 
015673,003048:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
015674,003049:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
015675,003050:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
015676,003051:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
015677,003052:    4227           75070                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
015678,003053:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
015679,003054:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
015680,003055:    4232           05211                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
015681,003056: 
015682,003057:    4233           05233        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015683,003058: 
015684,003059:    4234           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
015685,003060:    4235           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
015686,003061:    4236           00002                           TC       Q                                     
015687,003062:    4237           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              
015688,003063: 
015689,003064:    4240           11043        ISLIST+0           CCS      DSPLIST                               #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
015690,003065:    4241           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF DSPLIST = +0.
015691,003066:    4242           00002                           TC       Q                                     
015692,003067:    4243           05725        DSPABORT           TC       POODOO                                
015693,003068:    4244           21206                           OCT      21206                                 #  SECOND JOB TRYING TO GO TO SLEEP
015694,003069: 
015695,003070:                                                                                                  #  JAMTERM ALLOWS PROGRAMS TO PERFORM THE TERMINATE FUNCTION.
015696,003071:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES ENDOFJOB.
015697,003072:

015724,003099: 
015725,003100:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
015726,003101:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
015727,003102:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.
015728,003103:                                                                                                  #  ANY COMBINATION OF THESE BITS IS ACCEPTED.
015729,003104: 
015730,003105:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT IS RESTORED TO STATE IT WAS IN BEFORE BLANKSUB WAS EXECUTED.

015822,003197: 40,3453           11011                           CCS      MODREG

015832,003207:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED), TERMINATE VERB IS EXECUTED, OR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA VERB IS
015833,003208:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED.  IT WAKES UP JOB THAT DID TC ENDIDLE.
015834,003209:                                                                                                  #  
015835,003210:                                                                                                  #  IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0, IT PUTS +0 INTO DSPLOCK, AND TURNS OFF KEY RLSE
015836,003211:                                                                                                  #  LIGHT IF DSPLIST IS EMPTY (LEAVES KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF NOT EMPTY).

015977,003352: 
015978,003353:                                                                                                  #  IF MPAC, +1 ARE EACH +NZ OR +0 AND C(A)=-0, SHORTMP WRONGLY GIVES +0.
015979,003354:                                                                                                  #  IF MPAC, +1 ARE EACH -NZ OR -0 AND C(A)=+0, SHORTMP WRONGLY GIVES +0.
015980,003355:                                                                                                  #  PRSHRTMP FIXES FIRST CASE ONLY, BY MERELY TESTING C(A) AND IF IT = -0,
015981,003356:                                                                                                  #  SETTING RESULT TO -0.
015982,003357: 
015983,003358:                                                                                                  #  (DO NOT USE PRSHRTMP UNLESS MPAC, +1 ARE EACH +NZ OR +0, AS THEY ARE
015984,003359:                                                                                                  #  WHEN THEY CONTAIN THE SF CONSTANTS.)
015985,003360: 
015986,003361:    4431           54135        PRSHRTMP           TS       MPTEMP                                
015987,003362:    4432           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015988,003363:    4433           30135                           CA       MPTEMP                                #  C(A) +,  DO REGULAR SHORTMP
015989,003364:    4434           17257                           TCF      SHORTMP    +1                         #  C(A) +0, DO REGULAR SHORTMP
015990,003365:    4435           14433                           TCF      -2                                    #  C(A) -,  DO REGULAR SHORTMP
015991,003366:    4436           45035                           CS       ZERO                                  #  C(A) -0, FORCE RESULT TO -0 AND RETURN.
015992,003367:    4437           54154                           TS       MPAC

015996,003371:

015998,003373:    4444           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
015999,003374:    4445           05011                           WOR      DSALMOUT

016001,003376: 
016002,003377:    4447           45026        FLASHOFF           CS       BIT6                                  #  TURN OFF V/N FLASH
016003,003378:    4450           00006                           EXTEND                                         
016004,003379:    4451           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016005,003380:    4452           00002                           TC       Q                                     
016006,003381: 
016007,003382:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016008,003383: 
016009,003384:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016010,003385:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016011,003386:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016012,003387:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016013,003388: 
016014,003389:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016015,003390:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
016016,003391:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
016017,003392:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016018,003393:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016019,003394:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016020,003395:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016021,003396: 
016022,003397:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016023,003398:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
016024,003399:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
016025,003400:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016026,003401:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016027,003402: 
016028,003403:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
016029,003404:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016030,003405:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016031,003406:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016032,003407:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016033,003408: 
016034,003409:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016035,003410:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
016036,003411:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
016037,003412:                                                                                                  #  .
016038,003413: 
016039,003414:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016040,003415:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
016041,003416:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016042,003417:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016043,003418: 
016044,003419:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016045,003420:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016046,003421:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016047,003422: 
016048,003423:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016049,003424:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
016050,003425:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING
016051,003426:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016052,003427: 
016053,003428:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016054,003429:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
016055,003430:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016056,003431:    4456           04715        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016057,003432:    4457           10577                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016058,003433:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016059,003434: 
016060,003435:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016061,003436:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016062,003437: 
016063,003438: 04,2577                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016064,003439: 04,2577                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016065,003440: 
016066,003441: 04,2577           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016067,003442: 04,2600           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016068,003443: 04,2601           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016069,003444: 04,2602           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016070,003445: 04,2603           30001                           CA       L                                     
016071,003446: 04,2604           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016072,003447: 04,2605           05211        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016073,003448: 
016074,003449:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016075,003450:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016076,003451:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016077,003452:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016078,003453:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016079,003454: 
016080,003455:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016081,003456:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016082,003457: 
016083,003458:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016084,003459:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016085,003460:    4463           35016                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016086,003461:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016087,003462:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016088,003463:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016089,003464:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016090,003465:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016091,003466:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
016092,003467:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016093,003468:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016094,003469: 
016095,003470:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016096,003471:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016097,003472: 
016098,003473:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016099,003474: 
016100,003475:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
016101,003476:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
016102,003477:    4475           45016                           CS       BIT14                                 
016103,003478:    4476           00004                           INHINT                                         
016104,003479:    4477           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016105,003480:    4500           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016106,003481:    4501           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016107,003482:    4502           04504                           TC       +2                                    
016108,003483:    4503           04507                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
016109,003484:    4504           35035                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016110,003485:    4505           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
016111,003486:    4506           05215                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
016112,003487:    4507           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
016113,003488:    4510           45027                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
016114,003489:    4511           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
016115,003490:    4512           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              
016116,003491:    4513           35035                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016117,003492:    4514           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               
016118,003493:    4515           00144                           TC       RELRET                                
016119,003494:    4516           56002        RELDSP1            XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0.  NO DSPLIST SEARCH.
016120,003495:    4517           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  TURN KEY RLSE LIGHT OFF IF DSPLIST IS
016121,003496:                                                                                                  #  EMPTY.  LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF 
016122,003497:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST IS NOT EMPTY.
016123,003498:    4520           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016124,003499:    4521           04523                           TC       +2                                    #  +     NOT EMPTY.  LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE
016125,003500:    4522           04507                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  +0    EMPTY.  TURN OFF KEY RLSE LIGHT
016126,003501:    4523           35035                           CAF      ZERO                                  #  -     NOT EMPTY.  LEAVE KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE
016127,003502:    4524           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK

016236,003611: 
016237,003612:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
016238,003613:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
016239,003614:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
016240,003615: 
016241,003616:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
016242,003617:                                                                                                  #  
016243,003618:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
016244,003619:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
016245,003620:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.

016257,003632: 40,3526           71036                           MASK     DSPTAB     +11D                       #  TURNING OFF AUTO, HOLD, FREE,

016262,003637: 40,3533           65104                           AD       PRIO16                                #  EXISTS, THE ALARM WILL COME BACK.
